    #numbering unique index for each model in an easily function 
    def model_index(df, model_id='model_id', model_index='model_index'):
        last_model = ""
        model_index = []
        i = 0
        for model_id in df[model_id]:
            if model_id == last_model:
                i+=1
                model_index.append(i)
            else:
                last_model = model_id
                i = 0
                model_index.append(i)
        df['model_index'] = model_index
        return df

    model_index(midknight)

    #get the variation of the av size in each date of measure between all the models
    def min_max_to_avg(df):
        min_avg= []
        max_avg= []
        for row,k in df.groupby(['model_index']):
            min_avg.append(k['size'].min())
            max_avg.append(k['size'].max())
        min_max_avg= pd.DataFrame({'min':min_avg,'max':max_avg})
        return min_max_avg

    res= min_max_to_avg(midknight)
    print(res)

    #add 183 days to models from the southern hemisphere to compare in same dates
    #keep days from 1-365
    for index, row in rawdata1.iterrows():
        if any(substring in row['area'] for substring in ['chile', 'australia', 'new_zealand', 'RSA', 'mexico', 'india', 'venezuela', 'uruguay']):
            new_doy = row['doy'] + 183
            if new_doy > 365:
                new_doy = new_doy - 365
            rawdata1.at[index, 'doy'] = new_doy

    import datetime
    def avg_date(df):
        av_start_date= df['doy'].mean()
        start_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(str(int(av_start_date)), "%j").strftime("%d/%m/%y")
        print(start_date)

    avg_date(midknight1)
